# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

Perfect! I've created `/workspace/answer.json` with comprehensive findings about exponential backoff implementations across the three repositories.

## Summary of Findings:

**Kubernetes/kubernetes** - Core exponential backoff implementation:
- `wait.ExponentialBackoff()` function that retries conditions with exponentially increasing waits
- `Backoff` struct with Duration, Factor, Jitter, Steps, and Cap parameters
- Additional implementations in goroutinemap and webhook packages

**Grafana/grafana** - Multiple specialized retry implementations:
- `defaultGitRetrier()` - ExponentialBackoffRetrier for Git operations (8 attempts, 100ms→5s backoff)
- `retryWithBackoff()` - Uses Kubernetes wait package with configurable backoff
- `newExponentialBackoffRetryer()` - Alert scheduling retry with custom clock support

**Prometheus/prometheus** - Remote write queue backoff:
- `sendWriteRequestWithBackoff()` - Exponential backoff starting at MinBackoff (30ms), doubling until MaxBackoff (5s)
- Respects Retry-After headers from servers
- Prevents resharding during active backoff periods

The answer file includes all 8 source files, 12 key symbols, a call chain showing the main implementations, and a detailed narrative explanation of how each repository implements exponential backoff patterns.

The core function is `ExponentialBackoff(backoff Backoff, condition ConditionFunc)` which repeatedly executes a condition function with exponentially increasing waits between attempts. The `Backoff` struct defines parameters: Duration (initial wait), Factor (multiplier), Jitter (randomization), Steps (max attempts), and Cap (max wait time). For context-aware usage, `ExponentialBackoffWithContext` is provided for cancellable retry loops.\\n\\nAdditional exponential backoff implementations in Kubernetes include:\\n- `exponentialBackoffManagerImpl` (deprecated) in the same backoff.go file\\n- `ExponentialBackoff` struct in `pkg/util/goroutinemap/exponentialbackoff/exponential_backoff.go` for tracking operation errors\\n- `WithExponentialBackoff` methods in `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/util/webhook/webhook.go` for retrying webhook operations\\n\\n## Grafana - ExponentialBackoffRetrier\\n\\nGrafana implements exponential backoff retry logic in multiple places:\\n\\n1. **Git Repository Retrier** (`apps/provisioning/pkg/repository/git/repository.go`): The `defaultGitRetrier()` function creates an `ExponentialBackoffRetrier` configured with 8 total attempts (1 initial + 7 retries), initial delay of 100ms, maximum delay of 5 seconds, exponential multiplier of 2.0, and jitter enabled. This retries network errors, 5xx errors, and 429 rate-limit errors.\\n\\n2. **Provisioning Resources Retry** (`pkg/registry/apis/provisioning/resources/retry_client.go`): The `retryWithBackoff()` method uses Kubernetes' `wait.ExponentialBackoff` with a `defaultRetryBackoff()` configuration (100ms initial duration, 2.0 factor, 0.1 jitter, 8 steps, 5s cap).\\n\\n3. **Alert Scheduling Retrier** (`pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/retry.go`): The `newExponentialBackoffRetryer()` function creates an `exponentialBackoffRetryer` wrapping a `backoff.BackOff` implementation with configurable max retries, initial/max delays, randomization factor, and clock provider.\\n\\n## Prometheus - Remote Write Backoff\\n\\nPrometheus implements exponential backoff for remote write operations in `storage/remote/queue_manager.go`. The `sendWriteRequestWithBackoff()` function implements retry logic by:\\n\\n1. Starting with `MinBackoff` duration (default 30ms)\\n2. Doubling the backoff on each recoverable error\\n3. Capping at `MaxBackoff` (default 5s)\\n4. Respecting Retry-After headers when provided by the server\\n5. Disabling resharding during active retry backoff to prevent thundering herd\\n\\nThe `QueueConfig` struct in `config/config.go` defines these backoff parameters alongside retry configuration.\\n\"\n}\n",
